<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ نُوحٍ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مَالَكُمْ لَاتَرْجُونَ لِلّٰهِ وَقَارًاۚ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَقَدْ خَلَقَكُمْ اَطْوَارًا ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ تَرَوْا كَيْفَ خَلَقَ اللّٰهُ سَبْعَ سَمٰوَاتٍ طِبَاقًاۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَعَلَ الْقَمَرَ ف۪يهِنَّ نُورًا وَجَعَلَ الشَّمْسَ سِرَاجًا ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاللّٰهُ اَنْبَتَكُمْ مِنَ الْاَرْضِ نَبَاتًاۙ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ يُع۪يدُكُمْ ف۪يهَا وَيُخْرِجُكُمْ اِخْرَاجًا ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاللّٰهُ جَعَلَ لَكُمُ الْاَرْضَ بِسَاطًاۙ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِتَسْلُكُوا مِنْهَا سُبُلاً فِجَاجًا۟ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْجِنِّ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُلْ اُو۫حِىَ اِلَىَّ اَنَّهُ اسْتَمَعَ نَفَرٌ مِنَ الْجِنِّ فَقَالُٓوا اِنَّا سَمِعْنَا قُرْاٰنًا عَجَبًاۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَهْد۪ٓى اِلَى الرُّشْدِ فَاٰمَنَّا بِه۪ۜ وَلَنْ نُشْرِكَ بِرَبِّنَٓا اَحَدًاۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَنَّهُ تَعَالٰى جَدُّ رَبِّنَا مَااتَّخَذَ صَاحِبَةً وَلَا وَلَدًاۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَنَّهُ كَانَ يَقُولُ سَف۪يهُنَا عَلَى اللّٰهِ شَطَطًاۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَنَّا ظَنَنَّٓا اَنْ لَنْ تَقُولَ اْلاِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ عَلَى اللّٰهِ كَذِبًاۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْمُزَّمِّلِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَٓا اَيُّهَا الْمُزَّمِّلُۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُمِ الَّيْلَ اِلَّا قَل۪يلاًۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">نِصْفَهُٓ اَوِ انْقُصْ مِنْهُ قَل۪يلاًۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَوْ زِدْ عَلَيْهِ وَرَتِّلِ الْقُرْاٰنَ تَرْت۪يلاًۜ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّا سَنُلْق۪ى عَلَيْكَ قَوْلاً ثَق۪يلاًۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ نَاشِئَةَ الَّيْلِ هِىَ اَشَدُّ وَطْئًا وَاَقْوَمُ ق۪يلاًۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ لَكَ فِى النَّهَارِ سَبْحًا طَو۪يلاًۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاذْكُرِ اسْمَ رَبِّكَ وَتَبَتَّلْ اِلَيْهِ تَبْت۪يلاًۜ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">رَبُّ الْمَشْرِقِ وَالْمَغْرِبِ لَٓا اِلٰهَ اِلَّا هُوَ فَاتَّخِذْهُ وَك۪يلاً ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاصْبِرْ عَلٰى مَايَقُولُونَ وَاهْجُرْهُمْ هَجْرًا جَم۪يلاً ﴿١٠﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْمُدَّثِّرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَٓا اَيُّهَا الْمُدَّثِّرُۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُمْ فَاَنْذِرْۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَرَبَّكَ فَكَبِّرْۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَثِيَابَكَ فَطَهِّرْۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالرُّجْزَ فَاهْجُرْۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَا تَمْنُنْ تَسْتَكْثِرُۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلِرَبِّكَ فَاصْبِرْۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْقِيٰمَةِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَٓا اُقْسِمُ بِيَوْمِ الْقِيٰمَةِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَٓا اُقْسِمُ بِالنَّفْسِ اللَّوَّامَةِ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَيَحْسَبُ اْلاِنْسَانُ اَلَّنْ نَجْمَعَ عِظَامَهُۜ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلٰى قَادِر۪ينَ عَلٰٓى اَنْ نُسَوِّىَ بَنَانَهُ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلْ يُر۪يدُ اْلاِنْسَانُ لِيَفْجُرَ اَمَامَهُۚ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَسْئَلُ اَيَّانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيٰمَةِۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا بَرِقَ الْبَصَرُۙ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَخَسَفَ الْقَمَرُۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجُمِعَ الشَّمْسُ وَالْقَمَرُۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَقُولُ اْلاِنْسَانُ يَوْمَئِذٍ اَيْنَ الْمَفَرُّ ۚ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّا لَا وَزَرَۜ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلٰى رَبِّكَ يَوْمَئِذٍ ۨالْمُسْتَقَرُّ ۜ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يُنَبَّؤُا اْلاِنْسَانُ يَوْمَئِذٍ بِمَا قَدَّمَ وَاَخَّرَۜ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلِ اْلاِنْسَانُ عَلٰى نَفْسِه۪ بَص۪يرَةٌۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَوْ اَلْقٰى مَعَاذ۪يرَهُۜ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَا تُحَرِّكْ بِه۪ لِسَانَكَ لِتَعْجَلَ بِه۪ۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ عَلَيْنَا جَمْعَهُ وَقُرْاٰنَهُۚ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا قَرَاْنَاهُ فَاتَّبِعْ قُرْاٰنَهُۚ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اِنَّ عَلَيْنَا بَيَانَهُۜ ﴿١٩﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّا بَلْ تُحِبُّونَ الْعَاجِلَةَۙ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَتَذَرُونَ اْلاٰخِرَةَۜ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ نَاضِرَةٌۙ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلٰى رَبِّهَا نَاظِرَةٌۚ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَوُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ بَاسِرَةٌۙ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تَظُنُّ اَنْ يُفْعَلَ بِهَا فَاقِرَةٌۜ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّٓا اِذَا بَلَغَتِ التَّرَاقِيَۙ ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَق۪يلَ مَنْ۔ رَاقٍۙ ﴿٢٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَظَنَّ اَنَّهُ الْفِرَاقُۙ ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْتَفَّتِ السَّاقُ بِالسَّاقِۙ ﴿٢٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلٰى رَبِّكَ يَوْمَئِذٍ ۨالْمَسَاقُۜ ۟ ﴿٣٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَلَا صَدَّقَ وَلَا صَلّٰىۙ ﴿٣١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلٰكِنْ كَذَّبَ وَتَوَلّٰىۙ ﴿٣٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ ذَهَبَ اِلٰٓى اَهْلِه۪ يَتَمَطّٰىۜ ﴿٣٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَوْلٰى لَكَ فَاَوْلٰىۙ ﴿٣٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اَوْلٰى لَكَ فَاَوْلٰىۜ ﴿٣٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَيَحْسَبُ اْلاِنْسَانُ اَنْ يُتْرَكَ سُدًىۜ ﴿٣٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ يَكُ نُطْفَةً مِنْ مَنِىٍّ يُمْنٰىۙ ﴿٣٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ كَانَ عَلَقَةً فَخَلَقَ فَسَوّٰىۙ ﴿٣٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَجَعَلَ مِنْهُ الزَّوْجَيْنِ الذَّكَرَ وَاْلاُنْثٰىۜ ﴿٣٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَيْسَ ذٰلِكَ بِقَادِرٍ عَلٰٓى اَنْ يُحْيِىَ الْمَوْتٰى ﴿٤٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ اْلاِنْسَانِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">هَلْ اَتٰى عَلَى اْلاِنْسَانِ ح۪ينٌ مِنَ الدَّهْرِ لَمْ يَكُنْ شَيْئًا مَذْكُورًا ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّا خَلَقْنَا اْلاِنْسَانَ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ اَمْشَاجٍۗ نَبْتَل۪يهِ فَجَعَلْنَاهُ سَم۪يعًا بَص۪يرًا ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّا هَدَيْنَاهُ السَّب۪يلَ اِمَّا شَاكِرًا وَاِمَّا كَفُورًا ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّٓا اَعْتَدْنَا لِلْكَافِر۪ينَ سَلَاسِلاَ۬ وَاَغْلَالاً وَسَع۪يرًا ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ الْاَبْرَارَ يَشْرَبُونَ مِنْ كَاْسٍ كَانَ مِزَاجُهَا كَافُورًاۚ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَيْنًا يَشْرَبُ بِهَا عِبَادُ اللّٰهِ يُفَجِّرُونَهَا تَفْج۪يرًا ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يُوفُونَ بِالنَّذْرِ وَيَخَافُونَ يَوْمًا كَانَ شَرُّهُ مُسْتَط۪يرًا ﴿٨﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيُطْعِمُونَ الطَّعَامَ عَلٰى حُبِّه۪ مِسْك۪ينًا وَيَت۪يمًا وَاَس۪يرًا ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّمَا نُطْعِمُكُمْ لِوَجْهِ اللّٰهِ لَانُر۪يدُ مِنْكُمْ جَزَٓاءً وَلَا شُكُورًا ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّا نَخَافُ مِنْ رَبِّنَا يَوْمًا عَبُوسًا قَمْطَر۪يرًا ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَوَقٰيهُمُ اللّٰهُ شَرَّ ذٰلِكَ الْيَوْمِ وَلَقّٰيهُمْ نَضْرَةً وَسُرُورًاۚ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَزٰيهُمْ بِمَا صَبَرُوا جَنَّةً وَحَر۪يرًاۙ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مُتَّكِئ۪ينَ ف۪يهَا عَلَى الْاَرَٓائِكِۚ لَايَرَوْنَ ف۪يهَا شَمْسًا وَلَا زَمْهَر۪يرًاۚ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَدَانِيَةً عَلَيْهِمْ ظِلَالُهَا وَذُلِّلَتْ قُطُوفُهَا تَذْل۪يلاً ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيُطَافُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِاٰنِيَةٍ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ وَاَكْوَابٍ كَانَتْ قَوَار۪يرَاۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قَوَار۪يرَ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ قَدَّرُوهَا تَقْد۪يرًا ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيُسْقَوْنَ ف۪يهَا كَاْسًا كَانَ مِزَاجُهَا زَنْجَب۪يلاًۚ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَيْنًا ف۪يهَا تُسَمّٰى سَلْسَب۪يلاً ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيَطُوفُ عَلَيْهِمْ وِلْدَانٌ مُخَلَّدُونَۚ اِذَا رَاَيْتَهُمْ حَسِبْتَهُمْ لُؤْلُؤً۬ا مَنْثُورًا ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا رَاَيْتَ ثَمَّ رَاَيْتَ نَع۪يمًا وَمُلْكًا كَب۪يرًا ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَالِيَهُمْ ثِيَابُ سُنْدُسٍ خُضْرٌ وَاِسْتَبْرَقٌۘ وَحُلُّٓوا اَسَاوِرَ مِنْ فِضَّةٍۚ وَسَقٰيهُمْ رَبُّهُمْ شَرَابًا طَهُورًا ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ هٰذَا كَانَ لَكُمْ جَزَٓاءً وَكَانَ سَعْيُكُمْ مَشْكُورًا۟ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّا نَحْنُ نَزَّلْنَا عَلَيْكَ الْقُرْاٰنَ تَنْز۪يلاًۚ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاصْبِرْ لِحُكْمِ رَبِّكَ وَلَا تُطِعْ مِنْهُمْ اٰثِمًا اَوْ كَفُورًاۚ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاذْكُرِ اسْمَ رَبِّكَ بُكْرَةً وَاَص۪يلاًۚ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمِنَ الَّيْلِ فَاسْجُدْ لَهُ وَسَبِّحْهُ لَيْلاً طَو۪يلاً ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ هٰٓؤُ۬لَٓاءِ يُحِبُّونَ الْعَاجِلَةَ وَيَذَرُونَ وَرَٓاءَ هُمْ يَوْمًا ثَق۪يلاً ﴿٢٧﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">نَحْنُ خَلَقْنَاهُمْ وَشَدَدْنَٓا اَسْرَهُمْۚ وَاِذَا شِئْنَا بَدَّلْنَٓا اَمْثَالَهُمْ تَبْد۪يلاً ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ هٰذِه۪ تَذْكِرَةٌۚ فَمَنْ شَٓاءَ اتَّخَذَ اِلٰى رَبِّه۪ سَب۪يلاً ﴿٢٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا تَشَٓاؤُ۫نَ اِلَّآ اَنْ يَشَٓاءَ اللّٰهُۜ اِنَّ اللّٰهَ كَانَ عَل۪يمًا حَك۪يمًاۗ ﴿٣٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يُدْخِلُ مَنْ يَشَٓاءُ ف۪ى رَحْمَتِه۪ۜ وَالظَّالِم۪ينَ اَعَدَّ لَهُمْ عَذَابًا اَل۪يمًا ﴿٣١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْمُرْسَلَاتِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْمُرْسَلَاتِ عُرْفًاۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَالْعَاصِفَاتِ عَصْفًاۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالنَّاشِرَاتِ نَشْرًاۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَالْفَارِقَاتِ فَرْقًاۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَالْمُلْقِيَاتِ ذِكْرًاۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عُذْرًا اَوْ نُذْرًاۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّمَا تُوعَدُونَ لَوَاقِعٌۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا النُّجُومُ طُمِسَتْۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا السَّمَٓاءُ فُرِجَتْۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْجِبَالُ نُسِفَتْۙ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الرُّسُلُ اُقِّتَتْۜ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِاَيِّ يَوْمٍ اُجِّلَتْۜ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِيَوْمِ الْفَصْلِۚ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَٓا اَدْرٰيكَ مَا يَوْمُ الْفَصْلِۜ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيْلٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلْمُكَذِّب۪ينَ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ نُهْلِكِ الْاَوَّل۪ينَۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ نُتْبِعُهُمُ اْلاٰخِر۪ينَ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَذٰلِكَ نَفْعَلُ بِالْمُجْرِم۪ينَ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيْلٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلْمُكَذِّب۪ينَ ﴿١٩﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ النَّبَاءِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَمَّ يَتَسَٓاءَلُونَۚ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَنِ النَّبَأِ الْعَظ۪يمِۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى هُمْ ف۪يهِ مُخْتَلِفُونَۜ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّا سَيَعْلَمُونَۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ كَلَّا سَيَعْلَمُونَ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ نَجْعَلِ الْاَرْضَ مِهَادًاۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْجِبَالَ اَوْتَادًا۬ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَخَلَقْنَاكُمْ اَزْوَاجًاۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَعَلْنَا نَوْمَكُمْ سُبَاتًاۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَعَلْنَا الَّيْلَ لِبَاسًاۙ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَعَلْنَا النَّهَارَ مَعَاشًا۬ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَبَنَيْنَا فَوْقَكُمْ سَبْعًا شِدَادًاۙ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَعَلْنَا سِرَاجًا وَهَّاجًا۬ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَنْزَلْنَا مِنَ الْمُعْصِرَاتِ مَٓاءً ثَجَّاجًاۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِنُخْرِجَ بِه۪ حَبًّا وَنَبَاتًاۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَجَنَّاتٍ اَلْفَافًاۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ يَوْمَ الْفَصْلِ كَانَ م۪يقَاتًاۙ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ يُنْفَخُ فِى الصُّورِ فَتَاْتُونَ اَفْوَاجًاۙ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَفُتِحَتِ السَّمَٓاءُ فَكَانَتْ اَبْوَابًاۙ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَسُيِّرَتِ الْجِبَالُ فَكَانَتْ سَرَابًاۜ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ كَانَتْ مِرْصَادًاۙ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِلطَّاغ۪ينَ مَاٰبًاۙ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَابِث۪ينَ ف۪يهَٓا اَحْقَابًاۚ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَايَذُوقُونَ ف۪يهَا بَرْدًا وَلَا شَرَابًاۙ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلَّا حَم۪يمًا وَغَسَّاقًاۙ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">جَزَٓاءً وِفَاقًا ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا لَايَرْجُونَ حِسَابًاۙ ﴿٢٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَكَذَّبُوا بِاٰيَاتِنَا كِذَّابًاۜ ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَكُلَّ شَىْءٍ اَحْصَيْنَاهُ كِتَابًا ﴿٢٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَذُوقُوا فَلَنْ نَز۪يدَكُمْ اِلَّا عَذَابًا۟ ﴿٣٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ لِلْمُتَّق۪ينَ مَفَازًاۙ ﴿٣١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">حَدَٓائِقَ وَاَعْنَابًاۙ ﴿٣٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَكَوَاعِبَ اَتْرَابًاۙ ﴿٣٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَكَاْسًا دِهَاقًاۜ ﴿٣٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَايَسْمَعُونَ ف۪يهَا لَغْوًا وَلَا كِذَّابًاۚ ﴿٣٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">جَزَٓاءً مِنْ رَبِّكَ عَطَٓاءً حِسَابًاۙ ﴿٣٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">رَبِّ السَّمٰوَاتِ وَالْاَرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَاۙ الرَّحْمٰنِ لَايَمْلِكُونَ مِنْهُ خِطَابًاۙ ﴿٣٧﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ يَقُومُ الرُّوحُ وَالْمَلٰٓئِكَةُ صَفًّاۜ لَايَتَكَلَّمُونَ اِلَّا مَنْ اَذِنَ لَهُ الرَّحْمٰنُ وَقَالَ صَوَابًا ﴿٣٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ذٰلِكَ الْيَوْمُ الْحَقُّ ۚ فَمَنْ شَٓاءَ اتَّخَذَ اِلٰى رَبِّه۪ مَاٰبًا ﴿٣٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّٓا اَنْذَرْنَاكُمْ عَذَابًا قَر۪يبًاۚ يَوْمَ يَنْظُرُ الْمَرْءُ مَا قَدَّمَتْ يَدَاهُ وَيَقُولُ الْكَافِرُ يَالَيْتَن۪ى كُنْتُ تُرَابًا ﴿٤٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ النَّازِعَاتِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالنَّازِعَاتِ غَرْقًاۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالنَّاشِطَاتِ نَشْطًاۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالسَّابِحَاتِ سَبْحًاۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَالسَّابِقَاتِ سَبْقًاۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَالْمُدَبِّرَاتِ اَمْرًاۢ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ تَرْجُفُ الرَّاجِفَةُۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تَتْبَعُهَا الرَّادِفَةُۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُلُوبٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ وَاجِفَةٌۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَبْصَارُهَا خَاشِعَةٌۢ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَقُولُونَ ءَاِنَّا لَمَرْدُودُونَ فِى الْحَافِرَةِۜ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ءَاِذَا كُنَّا عِظَامًا نَخِرَةًۜ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قَالُوا تِلْكَ اِذًا كَرَّةٌ خَاسِرَةٌۢ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِنَّمَا هِىَ زَجْرَةٌ وَاحِدَةٌۙ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا هُمْ بِالسَّاهِرَةِۜ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">هَلْ اَتٰيكَ حَد۪يثُ مُوسٰىۢ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذْ نَادٰيهُ رَبُّهُ بِالْوَادِ الْمُقَدَّسِ طُوًىۚ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذْهَبْ اِلٰى فِرْعَوْنَ اِنَّهُ طَغٰىۘ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَقُلْ هَلْ لَكَ اِلٰٓى اَنْ تَزَكّٰىۙ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَهْدِيَكَ اِلٰى رَبِّكَ فَتَخْشٰىۚ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَرٰيهُ اْلاٰيَةَ الْكُبْرٰىۘ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَكَذَّبَ وَعَصٰىۘ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اَدْبَرَ يَسْعٰىۘ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَحَشَرَ فَنَادٰىۘ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَقَالَ اَنَ۬ا رَبُّكُمُ الْاَعْلٰىۘ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَخَذَهُ اللّٰهُ نَكَالَ اْلاٰخِرَةِ وَاْلاُو۫لٰىۜ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ ف۪ى ذٰلِكَ لَعِبْرَةً لِمَنْ يَخْشٰىۜ ۟ ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ءَاَنْتُمْ اَشَدُّ خَلْقًا اَمِ السَّمَٓاءُۜ بَنٰيهَا۠ ﴿٢٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">رَفَعَ سَمْكَهَا فَسَوّٰيهَاۙ ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَغْطَشَ لَيْلَهَا وَاَخْرَجَ ضُحٰيهَا۬ ﴿٢٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْاَرْضَ بَعْدَ ذٰلِكَ دَحٰيهَاۜ ﴿٣٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَخْرَجَ مِنْهَا مَٓاءَهَا وَمَرْعٰيهَا۬ ﴿٣١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْجِبَالَ اَرْسٰيهَاۙ ﴿٣٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مَتَاعًا لَكُمْ وَ لِاَنْعَامِكُمْۜ ﴿٣٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا جَٓاءَتِ الطَّٓامَّةُ الْكُبْرٰىۘ ﴿٣٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ يَتَذَكَّرُ اْلاِنْسَانُ مَاسَعٰىۙ ﴿٣٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَبُرِّزَتِ الْجَح۪يمُ لِمَنْ يَرٰى ﴿٣٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَمَّا مَنْ طَغٰىۙ ﴿٣٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاٰثَرَ الْحَيٰوةَ الدُّنْيَاۙ ﴿٣٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِنَّ الْجَح۪يمَ هِىَ الْمَاْوٰىۜ ﴿٣٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَمَّا مَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّه۪ وَنَهَى النَّفْسَ عَنِ الْهَوٰىۙ ﴿٤٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِنَّ الْجَنَّةَ هِىَ الْمَاْوٰىۜ ﴿٤١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَسْئَلُونَكَ عَنِ السَّاعَةِ اَيَّانَ مُرْسٰيهَاۜ ﴿٤٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪يمَ اَنْتَ مِنْ ذِكْرٰيهَاۜ ﴿٤٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلٰى رَبِّكَ مُنْتَهٰيهَاۜ ﴿٤٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّمَٓا اَنْتَ مُنْذِرُ مَنْ يَخْشٰيهَاۜ ﴿٤٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَاَنَّهُمْ يَوْمَ يَرَوْنَهَا لَمْ يَلْبَثُٓوا اِلَّا عَشِيَّةً اَوْ ضُحٰيهَا ﴿٤٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ عَبَسَ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَبَسَ وَتَوَلّٰىۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَنْ جَٓاءَهُ الْاَعْمٰىۜ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا يُدْر۪يكَ لَعَلَّهُ يَزَّكّٰىۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَوْ يَذَّكَّرُ فَتَنْفَعَهُ الذِّكْرٰىۜ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَمَّا مَنِ اسْتَغْنٰىۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَنْتَ لَهُ تَصَدّٰىۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا عَلَيْكَ اَلَّا يَزَّكّٰىۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَمَّا مَنْ جَٓاءَكَ يَسْعٰىۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَهُوَ يَخْشٰىۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَنْتَ عَنْهُ تَلَهّٰىۚ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّآ اِنَّهَا تَذْكِرَةٌۚ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَمَنْ شَٓاءَ ذَكَرَهُۢ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪ى صُحُفٍ مُكَرَّمَةٍۙ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مَرْفُوعَةٍ مُطَهَّرَةٍۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِاَيْد۪ى سَفَرَةٍۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كِرَامٍ بَرَرَةٍۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُتِلَ اْلاِنْسَانُ مَٓا اَكْفَرَهُۜ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مِنْ اَىِّ شَىْءٍ خَلَقَهُۜ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مِنْ نُطْفَةٍۜ خَلَقَهُ فَقَدَّرَهُۙ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ السَّب۪يلَ يَسَّرَهُۙ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اَمَاتَهُ فَاَقْبَرَهُۙ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اِذَا شَٓاءَ اَنْشَرَهُۜ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّا لَمَّا يَقْضِ مَٓا اَمَرَهُۙ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَلْيَنْظُرِ اْلاِنْسَانُ اِلٰى طَعَامِه۪ۙ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَنَّا صَبَبْنَا الْمَٓاءَ صَبًّاۙ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ شَقَقْنَا الْاَرْضَ شَقًّاۙ ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَنْبَتْنَا ف۪يهَا حَبًّاۙ ﴿٢٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَعِنَبًا وَقَضْبًاۙ ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَزَيْتُونًا وَنَخْلاًۙ ﴿٢٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَحَدَٓائِقَ غُلْبًاۙ ﴿٣٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَفَاكِهَةً وَاَبًّاۙ ﴿٣١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مَتَاعًا لَكُمْ وَ لِاَنْعَامِكُمْۜ ﴿٣٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا جَٓاءَتِ الصَّٓاخَّةُۘ ﴿٣٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ يَفِرُّ الْمَرْءُ مِنْ اَخ۪يهِۙ ﴿٣٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاُمِّهِ وَاَب۪يهِۙ ﴿٣٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَصَاحِبَتِه۪ وَبَن۪يهِۜ ﴿٣٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِكُلِّ امْرِىءٍ مِنْهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ شَاْنٌ يُغْن۪يهِۜ ﴿٣٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ مُسْفِرَةٌۙ ﴿٣٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ضَاحِكَةٌ مُسْتَبْشِرَةٌۚ ﴿٣٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَوُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ عَلَيْهَا غَبَرَةٌۙ ﴿٤٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تَرْهَقُهَا قَتَرَةٌۜ ﴿٤١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اُو۬لٰٓئِكَ هُمُ الْكَفَرَةُ الْفَجَرَةُ ﴿٤٢﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ التَّكْو۪يرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذَا الشَّمْسُ كُوِّرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا النُّجُومُ انْكَدَرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْجِبَالُ سُيِّرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْعِشَارُ عُطِّلَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْوُحُوشُ حُشِرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْبِحَارُ سُجِّرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا النُّفُوسُ زُوِّجَتْۙ ۬ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْمَوْءُ۫دَةُ سُئِلَتْۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِاَىِّ ذَنْبٍ قُتِلَتْۚ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الصُّحُفُ نُشِرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا السَّمَٓاءُ كُشِطَتْۙ ۬ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْجَح۪يمُ سُعِّرَتْۙ ۬ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْجَنَّةُ اُزْلِفَتْۙ ۬ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَلِمَتْ نَفْسٌ مَٓا اَحْضَرَتْۜ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَلَٓا اُقْسِمُ بِالْخُنَّسِۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلْجَوَارِ الْكُنَّسِۙ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالَّيْلِ اِذَا عَسْعَسَۙ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالصُّبْحِ اِذَا تَنَفَّسَۙ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُ لَقَوْلُ رَسُولٍ كَر۪يمٍۙ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ذ۪ى قُوَّةٍ عِنْدَ ذِى الْعَرْشِ مَك۪ينٍۙ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مُطَاعٍ ثَمَّ اَم۪ينٍۜ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا صَاحِبُكُمْ بِمَجْنُونٍۚ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَقَدْ رَاٰهُ بِاْلاُفُقِ الْمُب۪ينِۚ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا هُوَ عَلَى الْغَيْبِ بِضَن۪ينٍۚ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا هُوَ بِقَوْلِ شَيْطَانٍ رَج۪يمٍۚ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَيْنَ تَذْهَبُونَۜ ﴿٢٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنْ هُوَ اِلَّا ذِكْرٌ لِلْعَالَم۪ينَۙ ﴿٢٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِمَنْ شَٓاءَ مِنْكُمْ اَنْ يَسْتَق۪يمَ ﴿٢٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا تَشَٓاؤُ۫نَ اِلَّآ اَنْ يَشَٓاءَ اللّٰهُ رَبُّ الْعَالَم۪ينَ ﴿٢٩﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ اْلاِنْفِطَارِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذَا السَّمَٓاءُ انْفَطَرَتْۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْكَوَاكِبُ انْتَثَرَتْۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْبِحَارُ فُجِّرَتْۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْقُبُورُ بُعْثِرَتْۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَلِمَتْ نَفْسٌ مَا قَدَّمَتْ وَاَخَّرَتْۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَٓا اَيُّهَا اْلاِنْسَانُ مَا غَرَّكَ بِرَبِّكَ الْكَر۪يمِۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى خَلَقَكَ فَسَوّٰيكَ فَعَدَلَكَۙ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪ٓى اَىِّ صُورَةٍ مَاشَٓاءَ رَكَّبَكَۜ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّا بَلْ تُكَذِّبُونَ بِالدّ۪ينِۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِنَّ عَلَيْكُمْ لَحَافِظ۪ينَۙ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كِرَامًا كَاتِب۪ينَۙ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَعْلَمُونَ مَاتَفْعَلُونَ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ الْاَبْرَارَ لَف۪ى نَع۪يمٍۚ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِنَّ الْفُجَّارَ لَف۪ى جَح۪يمٍۚ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَصْلَوْنَهَا يَوْمَ الدّ۪ينِ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا هُمْ عَنْهَا بِغَٓائِب۪ينَۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَٓا اَدْرٰيكَ مَايَوْمُ الدّ۪ينِۙ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ مَٓا اَدْرٰيكَ مَايَوْمُ الدّ۪ينِۜ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ لَا تَمْلِكُ نَفْسٌ لِنَفْسٍ شَيْئًاۜ وَالْاَمْرُ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِلّٰهِ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْمُطَفِّف۪ينَ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيْلٌ لِلْمُطَفِّف۪ينَۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ينَ اِذَا اكْتَالُوا عَلَى النَّاسِ يَسْتَوْفُونَۘ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا كَالُوهُمْ اَوْ وَزَنُوهُمْ يُخْسِرُونَۜ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَا يَظُنُّ اُو۬لٰٓئِكَ اَنَّهُمْ مَبْعُوثُونَۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِيَوْمٍ عَظ۪يمٍۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ يَقُومُ النَّاسُ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَم۪ينَۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ اْلاِنْشِقَاقِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذَا السَّمَٓاءُ انْشَقَّتْۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَذِنَتْ لِرَبِّهَا وَحُقَّتْۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِذَا الْاَرْضُ مُدَّتْۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَلْقَتْ مَا ف۪يهَا وَتَخَلَّتْۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَذِنَتْ لِرَبِّهَا وَحُقَّتْۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَٓا اَيُّهَا اْلاِنْسَانُ اِنَّكَ كَادِحٌ اِلٰى رَبِّكَ كَدْحًا فَمُلَاق۪يهِۚ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْبُرُوجِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالسَّمَٓاءِ ذَاتِ الْبُرُوجِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْيَوْمِ الْمَوْعُودِۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَشَاهِدٍ وَمَشْهُودٍۜ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُتِلَ اَصْحَابُ اْلاُخْدُودِۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلنَّارِ ذَاتِ الْوَقُودِۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذْ هُمْ عَلَيْهَا قُعُودٌۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَهُمْ عَلٰى مَايَفْعَلُونَ بِالْمُؤْمِن۪ينَ شُهُودٌۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا نَقَمُوا مِنْهُمْ اِلَّآ اَنْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِاللّٰهِ الْعَز۪يزِ الْحَم۪يدِۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمٰوَاتِ وَالْاَرْضِۜ وَاللّٰهُ عَلٰى كُلِّ شَىْءٍ شَه۪يدٌۜ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ الَّذ۪ينَ فَتَنُوا الْمُؤْمِن۪ينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ثُمَّ لَمْ يَتُوبُوا فَلَهُمْ عَذَابُ جَهَنَّمَ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابُ الْحَر۪يقِۜ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ الَّذ۪ينَ اٰمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْر۪ى مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْاَنْهَارُۜ ذٰلِكَ الْفَوْزُ الْكَب۪يرُۜ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ بَطْشَ رَبِّكَ لَشَد۪يدٌۜ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُ هُوَ يُبْدِىُٔ وَيُع۪يدُۚ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَهُوَ الْغَفُورُ الْوَدُودُۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ذُوالْعَرْشِ الْمَج۪يدُۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَعَّالٌ لِمَا يُر۪يدُۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">هَلْ اَتٰيكَ حَد۪يثُ الْجُنُودِۙ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فِرْعَوْنَ وَثَمُودَۜ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلِ الَّذ۪ينَ كَفَرُوا ف۪ى تَكْذ۪يبٍۙ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاللّٰهُ مِنْ وَرَٓائِهِمْ مُح۪يطٌۚ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلْ هُوَ قُرْاٰنٌ مَج۪يدٌۙ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪ى لَوْحٍ مَحْفُوظٍ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الطَّارِقِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالسَّمَٓاءِ وَالطَّارِقِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَٓا اَدْرٰيكَ مَاالطَّارِقُۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلنَّجْمُ الثَّاقِبُۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنْ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ لَمَّا عَلَيْهَا حَافِظٌۜ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَلْيَنْظُرِ اْلاِنْسَانُ مِمَّ خُلِقَۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">خُلِقَ مِنْ مَٓاءٍ دَافِقٍۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَخْرُجُ مِنْ بَيْنِ الصُّلْبِ وَالتَّرَٓائِبِۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُ عَلٰى رَجْعِه۪ لَقَادِرٌۜ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَ تُبْلَى السَّرَٓائِرُۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَمَالَهُ مِنْ قُوَّةٍ وَلَا نَاصِرٍۜ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالسَّمَٓاءِ ذَاتِ الرَّجْعِۙ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْاَرْضِ ذَاتِ الصَّدْعِۙ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُ لَقَوْلٌ فَصْلٌۙ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَا هُوَ بِالْهَزْلِۜ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّهُمْ يَك۪يدُونَ كَيْدًاۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَك۪يدُ كَيْدًاۚ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَمَهِّلِ الْكَافِر۪ينَ اَمْهِلْهُمْ رُوَيْدًا ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْاَعْلٰى</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سَبِّحِ اسْمَ رَبِّكَ الْاَعْلٰىۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى خَلَقَ فَسَوّٰىۙ ۬ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالَّذ۪ى قَدَّرَ فَهَدٰىۙ ۬ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالَّذ۪ٓى اَخْرَجَ الْمَرْعٰىۙ ۬ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَجَعَلَهُ غُثَٓاءً اَحْوٰىۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سَنُقْرِءُكَ فَلَا تَنْسٰىۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلَّا مَاشَٓاءَ اللّٰهُۜ اِنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ الْجَهْرَ وَمَايَخْفٰىۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَنُيَسِّرُكَ لِلْيُسْرٰىۚ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَذَكِّرْ اِنْ نَفَعَتِ الذِّكْرٰىۜ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سَيَذَّكَّرُ مَنْ يَخْشٰىۙ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَيَتَجَنَّبُهَا الْاَشْقٰىۙ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى يَصْلَى النَّارَ الْكُبْرٰىۚ ﴿١٢﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ لَايَمُوتُ ف۪يهَا وَلَا يَحْيٰىۜ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قَدْ اَفْلَحَ مَنْ تَزَكّٰىۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَذَكَرَ اسْمَ رَبِّه۪ فَصَلّٰىۜ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بَلْ تُؤْثِرُونَ الْحَيٰوةَ الدُّنْيَاۘ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاْلاٰخِرَةُ خَيْرٌ وَاَبْقٰىۜ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ هٰذَا لَفِى الصُّحُفِ اْلاُو۫لٰىۙ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">صُحُفِ اِبْرٰه۪يمَ وَمُوسٰى ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْغَاشِيَةِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">هَلْ اَتٰيكَ حَد۪يثُ الْغَاشِيَةِۜ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَاشِعَةٌۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَامِلَةٌ نَاصِبَةٌۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تَصْلٰى نَارًا حَامِيَةًۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تُسْقٰى مِنْ عَيْنٍ اٰنِيَةٍۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَيْسَ لَهُمْ طَعَامٌ اِلَّا مِنْ ضَر۪يعٍۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَايُسْمِنُ وَلَا يُغْن۪ى مِنْ جُوعٍۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وُجُوهٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ نَاعِمَةٌۙ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لِسَعْيِهَا رَاضِيَةٌۙ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪ى جَنَّةٍ عَالِيَةٍۙ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَاتَسْمَعُ ف۪يهَا لَاغِيَةًۜ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪يهَا عَيْنٌ جَارِيَةٌۢ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ف۪يهَا سُرُرٌ مَرْفُوعَةٌۙ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَكْوَابٌ مَوْضُوعَةٌۙ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَنَمَارِقُ مَصْفُوفَةٌۙ ﴿١٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَزَرَابِىُّ مَبْثُوثَةٌۜ ﴿١٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَفَلَا يَنْظُرُونَ اِلَى اْلاِبِلِ كَيْفَ خُلِقَتْ۠ ﴿١٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِلَى السَّمَٓاءِ كَيْفَ رُفِعَتْ۠ ﴿١٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِلَى الْجِبَالِ كَيْفَ نُصِبَتْ۠ ﴿١٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِلَى الْاَرْضِ كَيْفَ سُطِحَتْ۠ ﴿٢٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَذَكِّرْ اِنَّمَٓا اَنْتَ مُذَكِّرٌۜ ﴿٢١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَسْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِمُصَيْطِرٍۙ ﴿٢٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلَّا مَنْ تَوَلّٰى وَكَفَرَۙ ﴿٢٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَيُعَذِّبُهُ اللّٰهُ الْعَذَابَ الْاَكْبَرَۜ ﴿٢٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ اِلَيْنَٓا اِيَابَهُمْۙ ﴿٢٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ اِنَّ عَلَيْنَا حِسَابَهُمْ ﴿٢٦﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْفَجْرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْفَجْرِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَيَالٍ عَشْرٍۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالشَّفْعِ وَالْوَتْرِۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالَّيْلِ اِذَا يَسْرِۚ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">هَلْ ف۪ى ذٰلِكَ قَسَمٌ لِذ۪ى حِجْرٍۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ تَرَ كَيْفَ فَعَلَ رَبُّكَ بِعَادٍۙ ۬ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِرَمَ ذَاتِ الْعِمَادِۙ ۬ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّت۪ى لَمْ يُخْلَقْ مِثْلُهَا فِى الْبِلَادِۙ ۬ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَثَمُودَ الَّذ۪ينَ جَابُوا الصَّخْرَ بِالْوَادِۙ ۬ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَفِرْعَوْنَ ذِى الْاَوْتَادِۙ ۬ ﴿١٠﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ينَ طَغَوْا فِى الْبِلَادِۙ ۬ ﴿١١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَكْثَرُوا ف۪يهَا الْفَسَادَۙ ۬ ﴿١٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَصَبَّ عَلَيْهِمْ رَبُّكَ سَوْطَ عَذَابٍۙ ۬ ﴿١٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَبِالْمِرْصَادِۜ ﴿١٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الشَّمْسِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالشَّمْسِ وَضُحٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْقَمَرِ اِذَا تَلٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالنَّهَارِ اِذَا جَلّٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالَّيْلِ اِذَا يَغْشٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالسَّمَٓاءِ وَمَا بَنٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْاَرْضِ وَمَا طَحٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَنَفْسٍ وَمَا سَوّٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاَلْهَمَهَا فُجُورَهَا وَتَقْوٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قَدْ اَفْلَحَ مَنْ زَكّٰيهَاۙ ۬ ﴿٩﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَقَدْ خَابَ مَنْ دَسّٰيهَاۜ ﴿١٠﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ اْلاِنْشِرَاحِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَمْ نَشْرَحْ لَكَ صَدْرَكَۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَوَضَعْنَا عَنْكَ وِزْرَكَۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ٓى اَنْقَضَ ظَهْرَكَۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَرَفَعْنَا لَكَ ذِكْرَكَۜ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِنَّ مَعَ الْعُسْرِ يُسْرًاۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ مَعَ الْعُسْرِ يُسْرًاۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَاِذَا فَرَغْتَ فَانْصَبْۙ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاِلٰى رَبِّكَ فَارْغَبْ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ التّ۪ينِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالتّ۪ينِ وَالزَّيْتُونِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَطُورِ س۪ين۪ينَۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَهٰذَا الْبَلَدِ الْاَم۪ينِۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا اْلاِنْسَانَ ف۪ٓى اَحْسَنِ تَقْو۪يمٍۘ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">ثُمَّ رَدَدْنَاهُ اَسْفَلَ سَافِل۪ينَۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلَّا الَّذ۪ينَ اٰمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ فَلَهُمْ اَجْرٌ غَيْرُ مَمْنُونٍۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَمَا يُكَذِّبُكَ بَعْدُ بِالدّ۪ينِۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَيْسَ اللّٰهُ بِاَحْكَمِ الْحَاكِم۪ينَ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْعَلَقِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِقْرَاْ بِاسْمِ رَبِّكَ الَّذ۪ى خَلَقَۚ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">خَلَقَ اْلاِنْسَانَ مِنْ عَلَقٍۚ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِقْرَاْ وَرَبُّكَ الْاَكْرَمُۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى عَلَّمَ بِالْقَلَمِۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">عَلَّمَ اْلاِنْسَانَ مَالَمْ يَعْلَمْۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">كَلَّآ اِنَّ اْلاِنْسَانَ لَيَطْغٰىۙ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَنْ رَاٰهُ اسْتَغْنٰىۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْقَدْرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّٓا اَنْزَلْنَاهُ ف۪ى لَيْلَةِ الْقَدْرِۚ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَٓا اَدْرٰيكَ مَالَيْلَةُ الْقَدْرِۜ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَيْلَةُ الْقَدْرِ خَيْرٌ مِنْ اَلْفِ شَهْرٍۜ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">تَنَزَّلُ الْمَلٰٓئِكَةُ وَالرُّوحُ ف۪يهَا بِاِذْنِ رَبِّهِمْۚ مِنْ كُلِّ اَمْرٍۙۛ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سَلَامٌ ۠ۛ هِىَ حَتّٰى مَطْلَعِ الْفَجْرِ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الزِّلْزَالِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذَا زُلْزِلَتِ الْاَرْضُ زِلْزَالَهَاۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَاَخْرَجَتِ الْاَرْضُ اَثْقَالَهَاۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَقَالَ اْلاِنْسَانُ مَالَهَاۚ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَئِذٍ تُحَدِّثُ اَخْبَارَهَاۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِاَنَّ رَبَّكَ اَوْحٰى لَهَاۜ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">يَوْمَئِذٍ يَصْدُرُ النَّاسُ اَشْتَاتًاۙ لِيُرَوْا اَعْمَالَهُمْۜ ﴿٦﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ خَيْرًا يَرَهُۜ ﴿٧﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ شَرًّا يَرَهُ ﴿٨﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْعَصْرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَالْعَصْرِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ اْلاِنْسَانَ لَف۪ى خُسْرٍۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلَّا الَّذ۪ينَ اٰمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ وَتَوَاصَوْا بِالْحَقِّ وَتَوَاصَوْا بِالصَّبْرِ ﴿٣﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْكَوْثَرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّٓا اَعْطَيْنَاكَ الْكَوْثَرَۜ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَصَلِّ لِرَبِّكَ وَانْحَرْۜ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِنَّ شَانِئَكَ هُوَ الْاَبْتَرُ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ النَّصْرِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِذَا جَٓاءَ نَصْرُ اللّٰهِ وَالْفَتْحُۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَرَاَيْتَ النَّاسَ يَدْخُلُونَ ف۪ى د۪ينِ اللّٰهِ اَفْوَاجًاۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">فَسَبِّحْ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّكَ وَاسْتَغْفِرْهُۜ اِنَّهُ كَانَ تَوَّابًا ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ اْلاِخْلَاصِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُلْ هُوَ اللّٰهُ اَحَدٌۚ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَللّٰهُ الصَّمَدُۚ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا اَحَدٌ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ الْفَلَقِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُلْ اَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الْفَلَقِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مِنْ شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمِنْ شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ اِذَا وَقَبَۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمِنْ شَرِّ النَّفَّاثَاتِ فِى الْعُقَدِۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">وَمِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ اِذَا حَسَدَ ﴿٥﴾</span>

<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">سُورَةُ النَّاسِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّح۪يمِ</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">قُلْ اَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِۙ ﴿١﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مَلِكِ النَّاسِۙ ﴿٢﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اِلٰهِ النَّاسِۙ ﴿٣﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِۙ ﴿٤﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">اَلَّذ۪ى يُوَسْوِسُ ف۪ى صُدُورِ النَّاسِۙ ﴿٥﴾</span>
<span class="quran-text font-arabic text-2xl text-amber-700 dark:text-amber-500 block text-center my-4">مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ ﴿٦﴾</span>
